***сахар.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сахар.html>са́хар</a> (2757)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">сахаръ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">saxarŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σάκχαρ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sákkhar</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σάκχαρι</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sákkhari</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σάκχαρον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sákkharon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pali" class="extiw" title="w:Pali">Pali</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="pi">सक्खरा</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="pi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sakkharā</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">शर्करा</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">śarkarā</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сахар.html>са́хар</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sáxar</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сахар.html>са́хара</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сахар.html>сахара́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сахар.html>сахаро́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sugar
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сахар.html>са́хар</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лает</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пища.html>пи́щу</a> вкусне́е, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обязательно.html>обяза́тельно</a> поле́знее.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Sáxar</b> délajet píšču vkusnéje, no ne objazátelʹno polézneje.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Sugar makes food tastier but not necessarily healthier.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коричневый.html>кори́чневый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сахар.html>са́хар</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">koríčnevyj <b>sáxar</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">brown <b>sugar</b></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>са́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>хар</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a−  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка) |  <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a> мн. ч. предположительны <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> неупотребимы.
</p><p><br />
</p>

<p><b>са́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>хар<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ца</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 5a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:производный.html>Произво́дное</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сахар.html>са́хар</a></b> ➔ <a href = vnd.unilang:сахар.html>са́хар</a> + <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ниц.html>ниц</a></b> + <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> (суффиксальный).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-сахар-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ниц</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сахар.html>са́хар</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sáxar</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сахарный.html>са́харный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sáxarnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)са́харнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)са́харней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sugar
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сахарный.html>са́харный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тростник.html>тростни́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sáxarnyj</b> trostník</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sugar cane</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сахарный.html>са́харное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:печенье.html>пече́нье</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sáxarnoje</b> pečénʹje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sugar cookie</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>rich in sugar
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сахарный.html>са́харная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>свёкла</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sáxarnaja</b> svjókla</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sugar beet</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sugary
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сахарный.html>са́харный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:фильм.html>фильм</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sáxarnyj</b> filʹm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sugary movie</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sensual</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the negative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sweet, pleasant, nice
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сахарный.html>са́харная</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">žiznʹ ne óčenʹ <b>sáxarnaja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">life is not so sweet</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сачок.html>сачо́к</a> (12209)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сак</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sak</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сачок.html>сачо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sačók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сачок.html>сачка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сачок.html>сачки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сачок.html>сачко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> butterfly net, hand net, net (for butterflies, insects or small fish)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> loafer, idler, shirker</li></ol>

***сбавить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сбавить.html>сба́вить</a> (16191)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ба́вить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-bávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбавить.html>сба́вить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sbávitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбавлять.html>сбавля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take off <i>(from)</i>, to deduct, to rebate, to discount
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сбавить.html>сба́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цена.html>цены</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sbávitʹ</b> s ceny</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to reduce/abate the price</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сбавить.html>сба́вить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вес.html>ве́се</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́ке</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sbávitʹ</b> v vése (o čelovéke)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lose weight</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбавить.html>сба́вить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спесь.html>спе́си</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sbávitʹ spési</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take someone down a peg or two</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбавить.html>сба́вить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тон.html>тон</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sbávitʹ ton</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to change one's tune, sing small</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбавлять.html>сбавля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sbavljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбавить.html>сба́вить</a></b>)

<ol><li>to take off <i>(from)</i>, to deduct, to rebate, to discount

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сбавлять.html>сбавля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вес.html>ве́се</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́ке</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sbavljátʹ</b> v vése (o čelovéke)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lose weight</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбавлять.html>сбавля́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тон.html>тон</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sbavljátʹ ton</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to change one's tune, sing small</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сбегать.html>сбега́ть</a> (4556)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bégatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбегать.html>сбега́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sbegátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбежать.html>сбежа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to run down (from)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сбегать.html>сбега́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лестница.html>ле́стницы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sbegátʹ</b> s léstnicy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run downstairs</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сбегать.html>сбега́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лестница.html>ле́стнице</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sbegátʹ</b> po léstnice</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run downstairs</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to run away, to make off, to flee, to break out</li>
<li>to escape</li>
<li>to elope</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбегать.html>сбе́гать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sbégatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to run <i>(to a place)</i> and get back, to run <i>(for)</i>, to go and get
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сбегать.html>сбе́гайте</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:врач.html>врачо́м</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Sbégajte</b> za vračóm.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Run for a doctor.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нужный.html>ну́жно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сбегать.html>сбе́гать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:магазин.html>магази́н</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mne núžno <b>sbégatʹ</b> v magazín.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I need to make a quick run over to the shop.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>сбе́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:гать.html>гать</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <p><b>сбе<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:гать.html>га́ть</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:сбежаться.html>сбежа́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>с-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-бег-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***сбежать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сбежать.html>сбежа́ть</a> (2893)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>бежа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bežátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбежать.html>сбежа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sbežátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбегать.html>сбега́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to run down (from)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сбежать.html>сбежа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лестница.html>ле́стницы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sbežátʹ</b> s léstnicy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run downstairs</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сбежать.html>сбежа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лестница.html>ле́стнице</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sbežátʹ</b> po léstnice</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run downstairs</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to run away, to make off, to flee, to break out</li>
<li>to escape</li>
<li>to elope</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>сбе<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жа́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <p><b>сбе<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>жа́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ться</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 5b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:сбегаться.html>сбега́ться</a>.
</p><p>1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> 2-е л. ед. ч. <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> употребительны семантически.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>с-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-беж-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сбербанк.html>сберба́нк</a> (17134)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Acronym of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сберегательный.html>сберега́тельный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:банк.html>банк</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sberegátelʹnyj bank</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбербанк.html>сберба́нк</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sberbánk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбербанк.html>сберба́нка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбербанк.html>сберба́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбербанк.html>сберба́нков</a></b>)

<ol><li>savings bank <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">financial institution</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>сбер<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:банк.html>ба́нк</a></b>

<p><b>сбе<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ре.html>ре</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:гать.html>га́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:сберечь.html>сбере́чь</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>с-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-берег-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сбережение.html>сбереже́ние</a> (13448)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сбере́г-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sberég-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбережение.html>сбереже́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sberežénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбережение.html>сбереже́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбережение.html>сбереже́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбережение.html>сбереже́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>(usually plural) savings</li>
<li>economy, saving</li></ol>

<p><b>сбе<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ре.html>ре</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>е</b>

Зализняка).

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:беречь.html>бере́чь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">beréčʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сберечь.html>сбере́чь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sberéčʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сберегать.html>сберега́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to save, to preserve</li>
<li>to spare</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сберкасса.html>сберка́сса</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sberkássa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сберкасса.html>сберка́ссы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сберкасса.html>сберка́ссы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сберкасса.html>сберка́сс</a></b>)

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>сбер<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка́с<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>са</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***сбивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сбивать.html>сбива́ть</a> (6587)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбить.html>сбить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sbitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-вать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбивать.html>сбива́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sbivátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбить.html>сбить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to knock down, to shake down, to cause to fall
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбивать.html>сбива́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спесь.html>спесь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sbivátʹ spesʹ s kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take smb. down a peg, to cut smb. down to size</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to knock down, to beat down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбивать.html>сбива́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цена.html>це́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sbivátʹ cénu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to beat down the price</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to put out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбивать.html>сбива́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>та́кта</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sbivátʹ s tákta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to to put out of time</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбивать.html>сбива́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:след.html>сле́да</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sbivátʹ so sléda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put off the scent</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбивать.html>сбива́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:толк.html>то́лку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sbivátʹ s tólku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bewilder, to confuse, to muddle</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбивать.html>сбива́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>пути́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:истинный.html>и́стинного</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sbivátʹ s putí ístinnovo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lead astray</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to tread down</li>
<li>to knock together</li>
<li>to churn</li>
<li><i>(eggs, cream)</i> to whisk, to beat up, to whip</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>сби<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:сбить.html>сбить</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>с-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-би-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ва</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>.
</p>

***сбить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сбить.html>сбить</a> (2607)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбить.html>сби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sbítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбивать.html>сбива́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to knock down</li>
<li>to cause to fall, to shake down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбить.html>сбить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спесь.html>спесь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sbitʹ spesʹ s kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take smb. down a peg, to cut smb. down to size</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбить.html>сбить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цена.html>це́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sbitʹ cénu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to beat down the price</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to put out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбить.html>сбить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>та́кта</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sbitʹ s tákta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put out of time</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбить.html>сбить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:след.html>сле́да</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sbitʹ so sléda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put off the scent</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбить.html>сбить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:толк.html>толку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sbitʹ s tolku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bewilder, to confuse, to muddle</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбить.html>сбить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>пути́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:истинный.html>и́стинного</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sbitʹ s putí ístinnovo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lead astray</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to tread down</li>
<li>to knock together</li>
<li>to churn</li>
<li><i>(eggs, cream)</i> to whisk, to beat, to whip</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сбиться.html>сби́ться</a> (5616)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбить.html>сбить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sbitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбиться.html>сби́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sbítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбиваться.html>сбива́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get off</li>
<li>to be aberrant</li>
<li>to go afield</li>
<li>to go astray</li>
<li>to be errant, to stray</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбить.html>сбить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sbitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
